411//------------------------------------------------------------------------------
412
413
414inline cFontPtr NEW_CFONT_CALIBRI_26()
415{
416 cImage *img = new chai3d::cImage();
417 cLoadPNG(img, CFONT_CALIBRI_26_BYTEARRAY, sizeof(CFONT_CALIBRI_26_BYTEARRAY));
418
419 cFontPtr font = cFont::create();
420 font->m_charset.m_base = CFONT_CALIBRI_26_CHARSET_BASE;
421 font->m_charset.m_lineHeight = CFONT_CALIBRI_26_CHARSET_LINEHEIGHT;
422 font->m_charset.m_width = CFONT_CALIBRI_26_WIDTH;
423 font->m_charset.m_height = CFONT_CALIBRI_26_HEIGHT;
424 font->m_charset.m_pages = CFONT_CALIBRI_26_CHARSET_PAGES;
425 for (int i=0; i<256; i++)
426 {
427 font->m_charset.m_chars[i].m_x = CFONT_CALIBRI_26_CHARSET[8*i ];
428 font->m_charset.m_chars[i].m_y = CFONT_CALIBRI_26_CHARSET[8*i+1];
429 font->m_charset.m_chars[i].m_width = CFONT_CALIBRI_26_CHARSET[8*i+2];
430 font->m_charset.m_chars[i].m_height = CFONT_CALIBRI_26_CHARSET[8*i+3];
431 font->m_charset.m_chars[i].m_xOffset = CFONT_CALIBRI_26_CHARSET[8*i+4];
432 font->m_charset.m_chars[i].m_yOffset = CFONT_CALIBRI_26_CHARSET[8*i+5];
433 font->m_charset.m_chars[i].m_xAdvance = CFONT_CALIBRI_26_CHARSET[8*i+6];
434 font->m_charset.m_chars[i].m_page = CFONT_CALIBRI_26_CHARSET[8*i+7];
435 }
436 font->m_charset.preProcess();
437
438 font->m_texture->setImage(std::shared_ptr<chai3d::cImage>(img));
439
440 return (font);
441}
